Website to show how My 2025 was, and what I did in it.

Welcome:






2025, a new year, 25 reminds me of technologies, innovations, and new things, I like this number a lot.
The photo of this year is very beautiful ❤️, little blue xD, it makes me think of spiritual evolution, connection with myself, inner peace, and happiness.
It also makes me think of good changes in the world, for the better, with people living better and with less conflicts and arguments.

Comment:

Título do episódio:
Yuru Camp△ EP08 "Provas, Caribou, Bolinhos, Delícia!" (Re-assistido 1x)

Tempo do comentário:
04:13 29/01/2025

00:08:
Tá bem frio mesmo ksks

00:22:
A Chiaki tá gripada, tadinha ksks
E querendo se esquentar com o saco de dormir, mas não tá ajudando muito ksks

00:37:
Se esquentar com fricção kkkkk

00:45:
Uma lagarta se contorcendo kkkkkkkkkkkk

02:31:
Que mesa pequena, é uma maquete de mesa de acampamento? kkkkk
E a tigela e a frigideirinha pequenas ksks
Acho que não serve muito pra sentar ao lado da mesa e usar pra comer
E sim pra cozinhar e preparar os ingredientes ksks
É mais pra ser chique com coisas pequenas, fáceis, e baratas mesmo kkkkk

03:04:
Que mesa linda, de metal ksks, e desmontável ainda, bem prática ksks

03:17:
Ela tentou juntar o conjunto, mas é minúsculo ksks

03:29:
A mesa foi 470 ienes (17 reais), pano de mesa 370 ienes (13 reais), almofada quente 190 ienes (7 reais)
Frigideira 460 ienes (17 reais), tigela de madeira 700 ienes (26 reais)
Garfo e colher 90 ienes cada (3 reais cada)
É um kit bem barato mesmo kkkk, o mais caro foi a tigela de madeira, que foi 26 reais (2025) ksks
No total ela gastou 2,370 ienes, que são 89 reais, bem barato kkkkk

03:47:
Ela é uma garota simples ksks, fica satisfeita com pouco ksks

03:54:
Japonês: "Niku kukai?"
Português: "Me diga, quer carne?"

Ela imitando o vovô classudo acampador que é o avô da Rin kkkkkk
E que na dublagem Brasileira também tem a voz do narrador kkkkk
Muito bom ksks

04:11:
A Nadeshiko mandando fotos aleatórias de onde ela mora kkkkk, em vez de estudar pras provas ksks
Um carro esquisito kk, é o carro do Google Maps kkkkkkkk, mapeando o local que a Nadeshiko mora ksks
A galinha atravessou a rua, um gatinho, um doguinho na picape ksks
O doguinho indo embora, e o Tsunayoshi kk

04:39:
A Chiaki gosta de viver sobre pressão kkkk, e estudar sobre pressão também ksks

04:56:
Ela sempre foi assim, sempre deixando pra estudar na última hora kkkkk

05:02:
Será que ela vai impedir a Aoi de voltar pra casa? kk

05:16:
Não pode colocar nada nessa tigela, mds kkkkkk
Vai comer só salada fria nela kkkk
Não pode colocar no fogo direto ou indireto, nem água ou comidas quentes ksks
É só pra preparar e temperar alimentos frios mesmo, como colocar temperos em carnes, saladas, legumes, e vegetais

Aviso:
- Não usar com comidas aquecidas, comidas com odores fortes, ou água quente.
Deformações ou rachaduras podem resultar na liberação de um odor de madeira.

- Não encharque em água.
- Não aqueça indiretamente sobre uma chama.
- Não exponha à fogo ou calor direto.

- Não aplique força excessiva.
Deformações, rachaduras, ou rupturas podem ser resultadas.

- Não utilize no micro-ondas, forno, máquina de lavar, ou secador de louça.

05:44:
700 ienes (26 reais) por uma tigela inútil dessa kkkkkk, só pra bonito mesmo ksks

06:01:
Então vai derreter o verniz e você vai comer verniz junto com a comida ksks, o que é tóxico pra saúde
E acho que sem o verniz a madeira fica áspera e mais frágil também
Então se for lavar com uma bucha dura pode raspar e cortar a madeira, tornando mais fácil o acúmulo de sujeira nas rachaduras

06:21:
Raspar com a lixa e azeitar a tigela, parece bom ksks

06:30:
Chiaki dublada: "Hora de lixar e azeitar!"

Kkkkkkkk, muito bom ksks
Mas pode ser depois das provas Aki? kk

06:38:
Essa Nadeshiko bocejando com a bocona aberta, parece que ela tá derretendo de sono kkkkkkkkkk
É tão engraçada e fofinha :3 ❤️

06:52:
A Nadeshiko-chan vai passar o ano novo na casa da vovó de novo :3

06:56:
Aya-chan, num lembro dela ksks

07:00:
Acampamento de Natal? (Kurisumasu)

07:03:
Chiaki é tão engraçada ksks, o jeito que ela fala é engraçado ksks
Alunos, na aula de hoje removeremos o verniz de uma tigela de madeira e temperaremos uma frigideira kkkkk
Ela não mencionou a segunda parte antes...

07:14:
Curar ou temperar é o processo de remover a proteção contra ferrugem de uma frigideira de ferro e cobrir ela com azeite de oliva
O que é a primeira coisa a se fazer com uma frigideira nova ksks
Eu não sabia disso, nunca tive uma frigideira de ferro kkkk
E elas estão aí fazendo isso enquanto tem as provas chegando ksks

07:40:
A Tahara-sensei vai tirar licença maternidade
E uma criança vai substituir a professora kkkkkk, mas é só na imaginação da Chiaki ksks
Parecendo um mangá kkkk

07:56:
Nessa parte, na dublagem Brasileira, a Chiaki fala:
"Mudando de assunto, lembra que falamos várias coisas da última vez que fomos acampar?"

No original em Japonês é:
"Por outro lado, lembra de como nós tivemos que andar muito na última vez que fomos campar?"

O original é maior que o dublado, então não caberia no time sync
A frase poderia ser adaptada para:
"Por outro lado, lembra que tivemos que andar muito da última vez que fomos acampar?"

Fica mais ou menos a mesma coisa, e sacrifica a naturalidade do "mudando de assunto" pra manter o sentido original da frase
Mas bom, realmente fica apertado adaptar a frase original, e isso eu entendo kk

08:07:
Só 100 ienes (3 reais) a ida da estação até o Parque Fuefuki??
3 reais? É preço de banana ksks

08:09:

A receita de hoje: Houtou

Lista de ingredientes:
(3 ingredientes por linha, 3 colunas, 4 linhas, 12 ingredientes no total, da esquerda para a direita, e de cima para baixo)
Cogumelos Maitake, Porco, Repolho Napa
Taros, Konjak, Tofu Frito

13:14:
Cenoura, batata, taro, e o caldo de dashi na panela
Na dublagem em Português eles traduziram o taro como inhame, mas na verdade era pra ser taro mesmo:
O taro (Colocasia esculenta) é um tubérculo com uma pele marrom e polpa branca ou creme
Enquanto o inhame (Dioscorea spp.) é um termo que se refere a várias espécies de tubérculos que podem ter uma pele que varia de marrom a roxa e uma polpa que pode ser branca, amarela ou roxa, dependendo da variedade.

13:19:
Aí quando os vegetais ficarem macios, é só jogar o macarrão na panela sem tirar a farinha
Ou seja, não pode lavar o macarrão, botar ele sem lavar ajuda a engrossar o caldo

13:28:
Depois de deixar de molho por algum tempo, coloca o resto dos ingredientes, e cozinha mais um pouco
E então coloca o missô ou miso Koushuu, que é tipo uma pasta de soja, arroz, ou cevada, que fez a água ficar laranja kkkk, se dissolvendo na sopa e distribuindo seu sabor umami

Pound cake, conhecido como bolo Inglês em alguns países, é um tipo de bolo que, tradicionalmente, é feito a partir de quatro ingredientes principais: 450 gramas de farinha, 450 gramas de manteiga, 450 gramas de açúcar e 450 gramas de ovos
O nome "pound" refere-se ao peso original de cada ingrediente na receita, que resulta em um bolo denso e amanteigado, ideal para acompanhar chá ou café

1 - I programmed in Python a little, coding my module Diary_Slim (01:36 04/01/2025):


Task number:
1

Task number by task type:
1

Task title:
I programmed in Python a little, coding my module Diary_Slim

Task type:
Python

When I completed the task:
01:36 04/01/2025

When I completed the task (UTC):
2025-01-04T04:36:11Z

Entry:
1. Python (01:36 04/01/2025)

States:
First task in year
First Python task in year

Task description:
I programmed in Python a little, coding my module Diary_Slim.

In the "Diary_Slim" module, I added the new methods "Define_Statistics", "Update_Statistics", "Update_Current_Year_Statistics", and "Verify_Input".
The "Define_Statistics" method defines the general statistics dictionary and for each year.
These statistics include things that I did during the year, like bike rides, driving, showers taken, times I washed my clothes, drawings, posted videos, work done, and family visits.
It creates these dictionaries with the data and writes the general statistics dictionary to the "Statistics.json" file, which is located in the data folder of the Diary Slim.
The method also defines a dictionary of years to store the folders and statistics dictionaries for each year.
After that, it iterates through the text dictionary of Diary Slim to find texts that contain the key "Add to statistics".
These texts have a list of custom statistics that will be added.
Then, the "Define_Statistics" method calls the "Update_Statistics" method to update the general statistics file, for all years, and update the "Current year" dictionary of Diary Slim, which will be used later.
The "Update_Current_Year_Statistics" method receives a modified statistics dictionary as a parameter, it updates the statistics file of the current year using that dictionary.
The "Verify_Input" method verifies what the user types.
It defines the input text to be shown to the user in their language.
Furthermore, it checks if the requested input needs to be an integer.
If so, it uses a regular expression to ensure that the input is indeed an integer.
Finally, I updated the "Define_Additional_Information" method to make it more modular.
This helps in defining statistics with responses of "Yes or no", "Type", and "Select".

The statistics have a main key, which is the name of the statistic in English.
For example, the Diary Slim text "Bike" corresponds to the key "Bike rides".
They can include questions, like "How many times did you drive the car?", and the expected type of response, which can be "Yes or no", "Type", or "Select".
Also, there is a dictionary of responses, in the case of "Yes or no", if the user answers "yes", it uses the "yes" dictionary that is inside the "Answers" dictionary.
For instance, if the question is "Did you create new websites?", and the answer is yes, it says "Type how many websites you create".
The statistics can also have additional questions, which are stored in a dictionary called "Questions".
For example, in the case of in-person work, the main question is "What is the name of the workplace?", and an additional question is "How much money did you earn?".
This way, the statistics can have multiple additional questions, each with its own statistic numbers.

In the "Write_On_Diary_Slim" sub-class, I modified the "Define_Item_Variables" method to include the option for alternative text formatting.
Normally, it is the root method "Define_Additional_Information" who formats the texts, in a simple way, just replacing the original text with a new formatted one.
But I needed something more flexible, like the ability to select items from a list to format, as well as using texts with different genders, based on a list that contains them.
For example, I have a text in Diary Slim that I use to register when my siblings come over to my house.
So, I select which sibling visited, and the method checks the gender of that sibling, based on two lists: one with male names, and another with female names.
Then, it formats the text that will be written in the Diary Slim, inserting the name of the sibling, and using "My brother" or "My sister", depending on the gender.

In the same sub-class, I created a new method called "Manage_Statistic" (Gerenciar_Estatística).
This method is executed when the Diary Slim text is also a statistic, and it retrieves the corresponding dictionary for that statistic.
If the statistic has a question, the method calls "Define_Additional_Information" to ask the user for the necessary information.
The responses can be "yes", followed by a question, "no", typing something, or selecting an option from a list.
Next, the method defines a statistic text in the user's language, which will be shown later, considering some conditions that may change which text will be used.
It also sets a key that will be used to locate the statistic in the current year's statistics dictionary.
The method creates a statistics dictionary within the "Text" dictionary of the root dictionary, containing the number of statistics to be updated.
Also, it includes the key "Dictionary", which contains a dictionary of the root statistic, with the text in the user's language, the old number, and the new number, which will still be changed.
This dictionary also has the key "Changed statistic", which has a default value of "False".
Then, the method sets the number to be added as one and checks if the statistic contains a question.
If it does, it tries to get the answer from the information dictionary, if the answer is a digit, it converts it into a number.
If the answer is "no" or zero, the number to be added is also set to zero.
If the key "Questions" is present in the statistic dictionary, the method iterates through the list of questions, sets the old number, and adds the root number to the current year's statistic number.
It also adds the additional statistics to the Diary Slim statistics dictionary, including the text, the old number, and the current number.
After that, the method counts how many statistics need to be changed and increases the statistic number using the amount of the number to be added.
If the old number and the new number are different, the method changes the state of "Changed statistic" to "True".
Then, it checks if there is a text decorator in the Diary Slim text dictionary.
If there is, it modifies the text that will be shown to the user, using the defined text decorator.
For example, if the normal text is "[Name of the Person]" and the text decorator is "Visits of", the text with decorator would become "Visits of [Name of the Person]."
This is a way to present the statistic text in a more appealing manner for the user.
After that, the method updates the statistics for the current year, using the local statistics dictionary that has already been modified.

The "Write" method checks if the Diary Slim text is a statistic and if it has been altered.
If both conditions are true, it sets a text based on the number: "Changed statistic" for a single statistic and "Changed statistics" for two or more.
Then, it displays this text along with the updated statistics.
The text for each statistic appears in the user's language, including " in [Current year]", the current number of the statistic, and " (before: [old number])".



2 - I programmed in Python a little, coding my modules Years and Diary_Slim (21:29 16/01/2025):

Task title:
I programmed in Python a little, coding my modules Years and Diary_Slim

21:29 16/01/2025

When I completed the task (UTC):
2025-01-17T00:29:39Z

Entry:
2. Python (21:29 16/01/2025)

Task description:
I programmed in Python a little, coding my modules Years and Diary_Slim.

On the "Years" module, on the main class and sub-class "Verify_Current_Year", I added the creation of files that I had to create manually before.
These were the files that I added:
Yearly statistics
This Year I (Personal version)
FutureMe

In the "Diary_Slim" module, I made the Diary Slim texts define their own statistics, inside each text's folder.
This way it is much more organized and modular, without having to define statistics in the Python module.
I moved the "Define_Additional_Information" and "Verify_Input" methods from the root class to the "Write_On_Diary_Slim" class.
I changed the "Define" part to "Get" in the first method.
I have greatly improved the way that the Diary Slim texts define root and statistics questions.
Now, all questions are in dictionaries "Question" and "Questions".
The question keys are now more or less the same, such as the question type key (Yes or No, Type, or Select).
In addition, there are also keys for the texts that appear when the user needs to type something or select an item from a list.

The "Get_Additional_Information" method now creates a dictionary of questions, adding each question to it.
If there is only one question, it puts it in the first position.
If there are more questions, it adds them all to the dictionary of questions, with their corresponding position keys.
After that, it iterates over the dictionary of questions, always checking the type of question (Yes or No, Type, or Select).
If it is "Yes or No", it asks the question and tries to find the answer in the dictionary of answers called "Answers".
Then, it stores the answer in the dictionary of user answers called "Response", formatting the answer and changing the text to be written, if necessary.
If it is "Type", it checks the user's input and stores that information in the "Response" dictionary.
If it is "Select", it sets the texts for the list item name and the type text.
Then, it asks the user to select an item from the list and stores that selection in the "Response" dictionary.
If the "Genres" key exists in the question dictionary, it formats the text to be typed with the selected item and a format text for the question, based on the genre.
Finally, it returns a dictionary with the text to be written, the dictionary of questions with their answers, and the state variable "Has questions".
I also changed the "Manage_Statistic" method to reflect the changes in the way the class handles questions, now using the new dictionary of questions.

In the "Write_On_Diary_Slim" class, I improved how the information for statistics with various questions is defined.
Now the "Manage_Statistic" method checks if the current question has the "Create sub-dictionary" key.
If it does, it creates a sub-dictionary using the user's response as the key.
It also checks if the current question has the "Add to sub-dictionary" key.
The method uses the value of that key to find the sub-dictionary and adds the user's response value to it.
Then, it updates the numbers with the values of the responses inside the statistics dictionary.
And it changes the text that will be written using a formatting text.
For example, I can work at the "Potatoes" company and earn money there.
Then, it would create a statistic sub-dictionary called "Potatoes", with the sub-keys "Days that I worked" and "Money that I earned".
I also created a new method called "Define_Money_Text".
It is used to define a text that will accompany a number that represents money.
For example: "$" in "$100" (normal version), and "dollars" in "100 dollars" (extended version).
The question dictionary needs to have the "Money" key for that method to be executed.
And it can have the "Use extended money text" key to use the extended version of the money text.
In the same class and throughout the entire module, I added monthly statistics.
This creates monthly statistics files, allowing for the registration of data for each month separately, rather than just the statistics for the entire year.

4. Python (21:13 19/02/2025)

Task description:

If the number of completed steps is equal to the total number of steps, it sets the "Completed non Christmas day steps" state to True.
Next, the method iterates over the list of date ranges and accesses the end date of each range.
If the end date is the 25th and the user has completed the steps that are not for Christmas days, the method checks if the current day is between the current date ranges, which are likely the 24th and 25th.
If this condition is True, it sets the state "Today is a chosen Christmas day" to True.
The method also displays today's date and sets the variable "calculate remaining time" to False.
If the "Current month is December" or "Today is in the first step date range" states are False, the method sets the end date to the date of the first step that is not for Christmas days.
If the state "Today is in the first step date range" is True and the state "Completed non Christmas day steps" is False, the method sets the initial text to talk about the execution of the steps that are not for Christmas days.
It also sets the final text to inform the user that they have completed all the steps that are not for Christmas days, as well as indicating on which day or day range the user should return to complete the steps for Christmas days.
It sets the end date to the date of the first step for Christmas days.
If the state "Completed non Christmas day steps" is True and the state "Today is a chosen Christmas day" is False, the method sets the end date to December 24th, indicating that the user should wait until that date to start their Christmas.
In addition, the method sets the initial text to inform that the user has completed all steps that are not for Christmas days, and that today is not a chosen day to celebrate Christmas.
If the state "Today is a chosen Christmas day" is True, the method sets the initial text to inform that the user's Christmas for the current year is beginning.
Then, it sets the final text to indicate that the user's Christmas is complete.
If the initial text is not empty, the method displays the text "Status of the Christmas steps" followed by the initial text.
If the "calculate remaining time" variable is True, the method displays the text "Wait until" and the defined end date.
Finally, it uses the new "Calculate_Remaining_Time" method to calculate the time difference between the current date and the end date.
-
In the "Execute_Christmas_Steps" method, I made the following changes:
I removed the opening of the planning file, which no longer exists.
If the state "Today is in the first step date range" is True and the state "Completed non Christmas day steps" is False, the method sets the step category key to "Non-Christmas day".
Conversely, if the state "Today is a chosen Christmas day" is True, it sets the step category key to "Christmas day".
The method uses the category key to obtain the list of steps pertaining to the defined category and then removes the completed steps.
The method iterates over the defined list of steps and displays the current step number, the total number of steps, and the step text in the user's language.
It retrieves the date range in which the step can be completed and displays this to the user, but only if the current range is not the same as the previous one.
This prevents the same date range from being displayed repeatedly, as happens for all steps that are completed on Christmas Day, which corresponds to the 24th and 25th.
If the step has methods, the method iterates over the step's methods dictionary, displays a space, and executes the method, passing the defined method value if it exists.
If the "Ask for input" state is True and the step is not the last in the list, or if the input text is present in the step's dictionary, the method waits for user confirmation before proceeding to the next Christmas step.
After the user input, the method marks the step as completed using the "Update_Steps" method.
If the "Ask to make a pause" state is present in the step dictionary, the method asks the user if they want to take a break and continue completing the Christmas steps later.
This is useful when the user wants to complete an important step on the 24th, but does not want to start their Christmas immediately.
If the user chooses to take a break, the method retrieves the text "Come back when you want to continue completing the Christmas steps for the {}!" and formats it with the end date of the current step.
The formatted text is then set as the final text, and the step loop is interrupted, not proceeding to the next step.
Finally, the final text previously defined in the methods is presented to the user.

In the "Open_Social_Network" sub-class of the "Social_Networks" module, I made the following changes:
Its "Define_Social_Networks" method now accepts a list of social networks that should not be opened.
This allows displaying the opening text and the social network link, as well as waiting for user confirmation with the input text before proceeding to the next social network, without actually opening the network.
This list can be useful, for example, to prompt the user to perform some action on the defined social network without opening it, such as when a social network is accessed via phone.
Additionally, the method now accepts a dictionary of input texts containing specific texts for each social network.
-
The "Open_Social_Networks" method has been updated to accommodate the new open definitions, checking the "Do not open" list and retrieving the specific input text for each social network, if any.
-
I also modified the "Show_Information" method to adjust the spacing and eliminate double spaces.

In the "File" utility module, in its root class, I created the new "Dictionary_2" method, which is the new version of the "Dictionary" method.
This method is capable of creating file dictionaries where the keys are lines terminated with a colon and the values are the subsequent lines.
Unlike the previous version, this new version can capture multiple lines to use as dictionary values, not just one.
The method also converts values that are lists into comma-separated or "and"-separated texts.
In addition, it can convert lists containing only one item to the item itself, depending on the parameter defined.

In the "Text" utility module, in its root class, in the "From_List" method, I added a new parameter called "genres".
This parameter accepts a list of genres, where each genre corresponds to an item in the list of items.
The genres are used to add the prefixes "of" to each item in the list, with the prefix depending on the genre of the item.
For example, with the list [Sunset Shimmer, Stake2], it would create the text "of Sunset Shimmer and Stake2", but in languages that are not English, it would add the prefix to all items.
